<script>
    /* Added Deferred and the code below to fix menu render problem */
    $("#menu1").kendoMenu();

    $(document).click(function (event) {
        var isMenuClick = false;
        if (!($(event.target).hasClass("menuheader") || $(event.target).hasClass("menuheaderrollover") || $(event.target).hasClass("k-icon k-i-arrow-s")))
        {
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; 8; i++)
            {
                if ($(event.target).closest('#menudropdown' + i).length)
                {
                    isMenuClick = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!isMenuClick)
            {
                hideopendropdowns(8);
            }
        }
    });
</script>

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__PayrollJobsAddendaDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__PayrollJobsAddendaDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'PayrollJobsAddendaDataView', GridHeight: '300', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__PayrollJobsAddendaDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__PayrollJobsAddendaDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '300', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__PayrollJobsAddendaDataView').click(function () {

        $("#settingsWindow__PayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__PayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'PayrollJobsAddendaDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__PayrollJobsAddendaDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__PayrollJobsAddendaDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__PayrollJobsAddendaDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_PayrollJobsAddendaDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "PayrollJobsAddendaDataView");

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___PayrollJobsAddendaDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("PayrollJobsAddendaDataView", "1");
                    GridSetSelectedItemsOn("PayrollJobsAddendaDataView", "");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__PayrollJobsAddendaDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__PayrollJobsAddendaDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__PayrollJobsAddendaDataView() {
        var gridName = 'PayrollJobsAddendaDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___PayrollJobsAddendaDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_PayrollJobsAddendaDataView');

        if (parseBool("False")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "PayrollJobsAddendaDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_PayrollJobsAddendaDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__PayrollJobsAddendaDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $('#UnselectAll__PayrollJobsAddendaDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#divPayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });

    showSpinner();
    function OpenJobBatchEditPopup() {
        $('#popupWindowJobBatchEdit').data("kendoWindow").center().open();
        $('#popupWindowJobBatchEdit').data("kendoWindow").refresh();
    }

    function onRefreshJobBatchEditPopup(e) {
        var jobType = $('#JobTypeDetail').val();

        e.sender.title("Job Batch Edit - " + jobType);
        RefreshPayrollRegisterJobBatchEditGrid(jobType);
    }
    function onCloseJobBatchEditPopup() {
        RefreshJobAddendaGridData();
    }

    function ClosePayrollRegisterJobBatchEditPopup() {
        $("#popupWindowJobBatchEdit").data("kendoWindow").close();
    }

    function SetPayrollRegisterId() {
        var d = { PayrollRegisterId: '642' };

        return d;
    }

    function PayrollJobsAddendaJobType_OnChange(e) {
        PayrollJobsAddenda_JobTypeChangedParentNotify();
        RefreshJobAddendaGrid();
    }

    function PayrollJobsAddenda_JobTypeChangedParentNotify() {
        try {
            var JobType = $('#JobTypeDetail').val();
            PayrollJobsAddenda_OnJobTypeChanged(JobType);
        }
        catch (e) { }
    }

    function RefreshJobAddendaGridData() {
        var grid = $("#PayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        grid.dataSource.read();
    }

    function RefreshJobAddendaGrid() {

        var JobType = $('#JobTypeDetail').val();

        if (this == $('#EmployeeName').data('kendoDropDownList')) {

            $('#EmployeeNumber').data('kendoDropDownList').select(0);
        }
        if (this == $('#EmployeeNumber').data('kendoDropDownList')) {

            $('#EmployeeName').data('kendoDropDownList').select(0);
        }

        var EmployeeNumber = $('#EmployeeNumber').val();
        var EmployeeName = $('#EmployeeName').val();

        var data = { JobType: JobType, EmployeeNumber: EmployeeNumber, EmployeeName: EmployeeName };
        var parm = $("#divPayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetDataViewParameters();
        parm.JobType = JobType;
        parm.EmployeeNumber = EmployeeNumber;
        parm.EmployeeName = EmployeeName;

        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/SetJobsAddendaFilters",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (data) {
                if (data == "") {
                    var grid = $("#PayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    $("#divPayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("AptaDataView").SetDataViewParameters(parm);
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }
            },
            error: function (e) {
                //
            }
        });
    }

    function OpenJobBatchEditPopupGrid() {
        var jobType = $('#JobTypeDetail').val();
        title = "Job Batch Edit - " + jobType;
        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divPayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection()
        var payrollRegId = 642;
        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowJobBatchEditGrid")
                .SetContent({ type: "POST", url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/RegisterJobBatchEditGrid", data: { aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, payrollRegisterId: payrollRegId } })
        .SetIsModal(true)
        .SetWidth(1020)
        .SetHeight(470)
        .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
        .SetonRefresh(function () { onRefreshJobBatchEditGridPopup(); })
        .SetonClose(function () { onCloseJobBatchEditGridPopup(); })
        .SetTitle(title);
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
    }

    function onRefreshJobBatchEditGridPopup() {
        var jobType = $('#JobTypeDetail').val();
        RefreshPayrollRegisterJobBatchEditableGrid(jobType);

    }

    function onCloseJobBatchEditGridPopup() {
        RefreshJobAddendaGridData();
    }

    function ClosePayrollRegisterJobBatchEditGridPopup() {
        $("#popupWindowJobBatchEditGrid").data("kendoWindow").close();
    }

<script>

    function onCloseJobOTDetailsPopup() {
        $("#divPayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
            url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/GetPayrollRegisterJobDC",
            dataType: 'JSON',
            success: function (result) {
                $('#tbAccountCodeEdit_PRItemDetailsacTextBox').val(result.dc.AccountCode);
                $('#tbAccountCodeEdit_PROTItemDetailsacTextBox').val(result.dc.AccountCodeOTAddenda);
                $('#GrossPay').data("kendoNumericTextBox").value(result.dc.GrossPay);
                $('#OT').data("kendoNumericTextBox").value(result.dc.OT);
                $('#GrossPaySalary').data("kendoNumericTextBox").value(result.dc.GrossPay);
                var textbox = $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PROTItemDetailsacTextBox");
                if (result.dc.MultipleOTRecords) {
                    $('#OT').data("kendoNumericTextBox").enable(false);
                    textbox.attr("disabled", "disabled");
                }
                else {
                    $('#OT').data("kendoNumericTextBox").enable();
                    textbox.removeAttr("disabled");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "PayrollRegister", "PayrollManagementDataView");

    function PayrollJobsAddenda_OnJobTypeChanged(jobType) {
        var btnBatchEdit = $("#btnBatchEdit__PayrollManagementDataView");
        var btnBatchEditGrid = $("#btnBatchEditGrid__PayrollManagementDataView");

        if (btnBatchEdit != null) {
            var batchEditDisabled = true;
            if (jobType.indexOf("Hourly") &gt;= 0) {
                batchEditDisabled = false;
            }
            else if (jobType == "Daily") {
                batchEditDisabled = false;
            }
            if (batchEditDisabled) {
                btnBatchEdit.addClass("k-state-disabled").prop("disabled", batchEditDisabled);
                btnBatchEdit.attr("disabled", "disabled");
            }
            else {
                btnBatchEdit.removeClass("k-state-disabled").prop("disabled", batchEditDisabled);
                btnBatchEdit.removeAttr("disabled");
            }
        }

        if (btnBatchEditGrid != null) {
            var batchEditGridDisabled = true;
            if (jobType.indexOf("Hourly") &gt;= 0) {
                batchEditGridDisabled = false;
            }
            else if (jobType == "Daily") {
                batchEditGridDisabled = false;
            }
            if (batchEditDisabled) {
                btnBatchEditGrid.addClass("k-state-disabled").prop("disabled", batchEditGridDisabled);
                btnBatchEditGrid.attr("disabled", "disabled");
            }
            else {
                btnBatchEditGrid.removeClass("k-state-disabled").prop("disabled", batchEditGridDisabled);
                btnBatchEditGrid.removeAttr("disabled");
            }
        }
    }

    function onActivateJobOTDetailsPopup(e) {
        LoadGridOnDemand__PayrollOverTimeAllocationDataview();

    function onCloseJobEditPopup() {
        var grid = $("#PayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        grid.dataSource.read();
    }

    function RemoveJob() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(RefreshOnRemoveJob)
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
    }

    function RefreshOnRemoveJob() {
        var aptaDV = $("#divPayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();
        $("#divPayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/RemoveJobFromRegister',
                 { aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDV.GetAptaDataViewSelection(), massOperationId: massOperationId },
                'JobBatchEdit', function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#PayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");

    }

        if ($("#divPayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
            ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm", "Are you sure you want to remove the selected job(s) from payroll?", RemoveJob);
        }
    });

    $("#btnMassDaysHours__PayrollManagementDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#PayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (NoItemsSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            return;
        }
        var aptaDV = $("#divPayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        var data = { aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDV.GetAptaDataViewSelection() };
        var JobType = '';

        aptaDV.MakeAjaxCall({
            url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/CanMassUpdate",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            error: function (xhr, status, error) {
                alert(error);
            },
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success == 0) {

                    ShowOkDialog("Notice", "Please select only one type of job (Daily or Hourly) to update.", null);
                }
                else if (result.Success == 2) {
                    ShowOkDialog("Notice", "Please only select Salary Time Sheet or Daily or Hourly type jobs to set mass days/hours.", null);
                }
                else {
                    setFocusEventForKendoWindow("popupPayrollMassDaysHours");
                    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupPayrollMassDaysHours")
                    .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/MassDaysHours?" + "JobType=" + JobType + "&amp;PayrollRegisterId=642" })
                    .SetIsModal(true)
                    .SetTitle("Set Mass Days/Hours")
                    .SetonRefresh(function (e) { setFocusToFirstEditCtrl("popupPayrollMassDaysHours", false); });

                    finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
                }
            }
        });

    });

    function EditPayrollRegisterJob(PayrollRegisterId, EmployeeId, CycleId, JobSequence, ItemSequence) {

        var id = PayrollRegisterId + '~' + EmployeeId + '~' + CycleId + '~' + ItemSequence + "~" + JobSequence;

        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divPayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();

        EditPayrollRegisterJobFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection);
    }

    function EditPayrollRegisterJobFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection) {
        var data;

        data = { id: id, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection };

        var finsWindow = $("#popupWindowJobEdit").data("FINSWindow");

        if (finsWindow == null) {
            finsWindow =
                FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowJobEdit")
                    .SetContent({ type: "POST", url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/RegisterJobEdit", data: data })
        .SetIsModal(true)
        .SetIsResizable(true)
        .SetWidth(770)
        .SetHeight('50%')
        .SetTitle("Job Edit")
        .SetonClose(onCloseJobEditPopup)
        .SetonDeactivate(function () { destroyACMultipleAllocationWindows("PRItemDetails"); destroyACMultipleAllocationWindows("PROTItemDetails"); })
        .SetClearWindowOnClose(true)
        .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true);
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        }
        else {

            finsWindow.SetTitle("Job Edit").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/RegisterJobEdit", data: data, type: "POST" });
            finsWindow.OpenWindow();
        }
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("PayrolRegisterJobEditDataView", "PayrolRegisterJobEditDataView", null);

    }

    function SaveRegister() {

        var PayrollPeriodId = $("#PayrollPeriodId").val();
        var TransactionDate = $("#TransactionDate").val();
        var PayDate = $("#PayDate").val();
        var RegisterType = $("#RegisterType").val();

        var validationMessage = '';

        if (typeof PayrollPeriodId == 'undefined' || PayrollPeriodId == '')
            validationMessage += 'Payroll Period is required.' + '&lt;br /&gt;';

        if (typeof TransactionDate == 'undefined' || TransactionDate == '')
            validationMessage += 'Transaction Date is required.' + '&lt;br /&gt;';

        if (typeof PayDate == 'undefined' || PayDate == '')
            validationMessage += 'Pay Date is required.' + '&lt;br /&gt;';

        if (typeof RegisterType == 'undefined' || RegisterType == '')
            validationMessage += 'Register Type is required.' + '&lt;br /&gt;';

        if (validationMessage != '') {

            ShowAjaxMessage(validationMessage, "error");
            return;
        }

        var form = $("#FormPayrollRegister");

        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/Save",
            data: form.serialize(),
            success: function (result) {
                if (result.Success === true) {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                    if (result.NewRegister) {
                        window.location.href = "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/RegisterDetails" + "?id=" + result.PayrollRegisterId + "&amp;addMode=" + result.NewRegister;
                    }
                    else {
                        window.location.href = "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/RegisterDetails" + "?id=" + result.PayrollRegisterId;
                    }
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                }
            },
            error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
            }
        });
    }

    function btnSave__PayrollRegister() {

        var useSupplementalTaxRateOld = $("#UseSupplementalTaxRateOld").val();
        var useSupplementalTaxRate = $("#UseSupplementalTaxRate").is(':checked');
        if (useSupplementalTaxRate) {
            if (useSupplementalTaxRate.toString().toUpperCase() !== useSupplementalTaxRateOld.toUpperCase()) {
                ShowYesNoCancelDialog("Confirm", "You have chosen this register to use the Supplemental Tax Rate for Federal and State Withholding Tax (if applicable). This will charge tax at the Supplemental rate, and not at the rate of the employees’ deduction sets.&amp;#160; Are you sure you wish to continue this register with the Supplemental Tax Rate?"
                    , function () {
                        SaveRegister();
                    }
                    , function () {
                        $("#UseSupplementalTaxRate").prop('checked', false);
                        SaveRegister();
                    });
            }
            else {
                SaveRegister();
            }
        }
        else {
            SaveRegister();
        }
    }

    function PayrollCycleChange() {
        //ajax call with period id to get transaction data(period end date) and pay date(from periodpaydate field)

        var pcid = $("#PayrollCycleList").val();

        if (pcid == "") {
            pcid = -1;
        }

        var data = {
            PayrollCycleId: pcid
        };

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/GetPayrollPeriodsByPayrollCycle',
            cache: false,
            data: data,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            success: function (result) {
                //debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    var dropdownlist = $("#PayrollPeriodId").data("kendoDropDownList");
                    dropdownlist.setDataSource(result);
                    dropdownlist.refresh();
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function PeriodChange() {
        //ajax call with period id to get transaction data(period end date) and pay date(from periodpaydate field)
        var data = {
            PayrollPeriodId: $("#PayrollPeriodId").val()
        };

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/GetDataByPeriodId',
            cache: false,
            data: data,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            success: function (result) {

                if (result != null) {
                    //debugger;
                    //TransactionDate
                    if (result.TransactionDate != null &amp;&amp; result.TransactionDate != '')
                        $("#TransactionDate").data("kendoDatePicker").value(result.TransactionDate);
                    //PayDate
                    if (result.PayDate != null &amp;&amp; result.PayDate != '')
                        $("#PayDate").data("kendoDatePicker").value(result.PayDate);

                }
            }
        });
    }

    var payrollRegisterId = "642";
    if (payrollRegisterId &gt; 0) {
        var registerStatus = "New";
        if (registerStatus != "" &amp;&amp; registerStatus != "New") {
            $('#RegisterType').disable();
            $('#PayrollPeriodId').disable();
            $('#RegisterNumber').disable();
            $('#RegisterDescription').disable();
            $('#PayDate').disable();
            $('#TransactionDate').disable();

        }

        if (!(registerStatus == "Paid" || registerStatus == "Void" || registerStatus == "New")) {
            $('#btnSave__PayrollRegister').hide();
        }

        if (registerStatus == "Paid" || registerStatus == "Void") {
            $("#PayInCycle").disable();
        }
    }

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).click(function (event) {

            if (event.target.id == "btnMoreButtons" || event.target.parentNode.id == "btnMoreButtons") {
                event.preventDefault();
                showHideMoreButtons();
            }
            else {
                if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    document.getElementById("dvMoreButtons").style.display = "none";
                }
            }
            if (event.target.classList.contains('btnDetailMoreButtons') || (event.target.parentNode != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList.contains("btnDetailMoreButtons"))) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var id = event.target.id;
                if (event.target.id == "") {
                    id = event.target.parentNode.id;
                }
                showHideDetailMoreButtons(id);
            }
            else {
                if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                        $(this).css('display', 'none');
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                ShowMoreMenu();
            }
            if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).css('display') != 'none') {
                        ShowDetailMoreMenu(this.id);
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        $(window).resize(function () {
            ResetDivMoreButtonOnResize();
        });

        var _jobQueueNotificationTimer;

        function StartJobQueueNotifications() {
            if (_jobQueueNotificationTimer == null)
                CheckJobQueueNotifications('/QAAutom/Home/CheckJobQueueStatus');
        }

        function DismissJobQueueNotification(jobQueueID) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                async: false,
                data: { jobQueueID: jobQueueID },
                dataType: "json",
                url: '/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/DismissJobQueueStatus',
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Message != "") {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().ShowJobQueueNotification(result.TempData, result.Message)
                    } else {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().hide();
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    </script>


<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        FINSUI.FINSUIElement.setAptaFundBaseURL("/QAAutom/controller/action", true);
        

        if ('Detail' == "Detail") {
            doStickyButtons();
        }
        registerFINSComboBoxEvents();
        $("body").find("input, textarea, select, span[role=listbox]").filter(":visible:not([disabled]):not([readonly]):not([tabindex=-1]):first").focus();

    });

    function doStickyButtons() {
        var sticky_button_offset_top = $('#menuhr').offset().top;

        // our function that decides weather the navigation bar should have "fixed" css position or not.
        var sticky_button_navigation = function () {
            var scroll_top = $(window).scrollTop(); // our current vertical position from the top
            var screenwidth = $(window).width();
            var buttonswidth = $('#actionbuttons').width();
            var buttonsheight = $('#actionbuttons').height();

            // if we've scrolled more than the navigation, change its position to fixed to stick to top,
            // otherwise change it back to relative
            if (scroll_top &gt; sticky_button_offset_top) {
                $('#menuhr').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 0, 'left': 40, 'z-index': 11, 'width': (screenwidth - 80) });
                $('#actionbuttons').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 10, 'right': 48, 'z-index': 12, 'width': buttonswidth });
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').css({ 'height': buttonsheight });
            } else {
                $('#menuhr').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttons').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').removeAttr('style');
            }
        };

        // run our function on load
        sticky_button_navigation();

        // and run it again every time you scroll
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            sticky_button_navigation();
        });
    }

    
    function registerFINSComboBoxEvents() {
        $('.FINSComboBox').each(function () {
            var kendoCombo = $(this).data("kendoComboBox");
            if (kendoCombo != null) {

                kendoCombo.bind("select", function (e) {
                    if (e.item != null) {
                        var dataItem = this.dataItem(e.item.index());
                        if (dataItem.Value == -999) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                }
               );

            }
        });
    }

<script>
    function OnEmployeeSelectionChange() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        var data = {
            EmployeeId: $("#SelectedEmployees").data("kendoComboBox").value(),
            PayrollRegisterId: '642'
        };

        var employeeId = $("#SelectedEmployees").data("kendoComboBox").value() == "[All Employees]" ? -1 : $("#SelectedEmployees").data("kendoComboBox").value();

        if (!$('#IsSupplemental').is(":checked")){
            $("#JobName").data("kendoComboBox").value('');

            var ddlJobName = $("#JobName").data("FINSComboBox");

            ddlJobName.DataParameters.CycleId = '5';
            ddlJobName.DataParameters.IsSupplemental = $('#IsSupplemental').is(":checked");
            ddlJobName.DataParameters.EmployeeId = employeeId;
            ddlJobName.DataParameters.PayrollRegisterId = '642';
            $("#JobName").data("kendoComboBox").dataSource.read();
        }

        if ($('#IsSupplemental').is(":checked") == true) {
            $("#CopyFromJobList").data("kendoComboBox").value('')
            $("#CopyFromJobList").data("FINSComboBox").DataParameters.CycleId = '5';
            $("#CopyFromJobList").data("FINSComboBox").DataParameters.EmployeeId = employeeId;
            $("#CopyFromJobList").data("kendoComboBox").dataSource.read();
        }
    }
    function OnJobNameSelectionChange() {
        GetRegionalFieldsRegisterJobView();
    }

    function OnJobTypeChange() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        HideShowJobTypePanels();
        var jobType = $('#JobType').data('kendoComboBox').value();
        $("#AccountCodeAmount").val('');
    }
    function CopyFromJobChange() {
        var employeeId = $("#SelectedEmployees").data("kendoComboBox").value();
        var jobId = $("#CopyFromJobList").data("kendoComboBox").value();
        var cycleId = $("#CycleId").val();

        if(jobId=="" || employeeId==""|| cycleId=="")
        {
            return;
        }

        var data = {
            employeeId: employeeId,
            jobSequence: jobId,
            cycleId: cycleId
        };
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/GetCopyFromJobList",
            data: data,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null) {

                    $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox").SetValue(result.AccountCode);
                    $("#hdnAccountStagingId_MultipleAccountCodeGrid_PayrollAddJob").val(result.StagigndId);
                    $("#AccountStagingId").val(result.StagigndId);
                    if(result.AccountCode !='Multiple')
                    {
                        SetLabelDescriptionAccountCode('lblAccountDesc_PayrollAddJobacTextBox', result.AccountCode);
                    }
                    $("#CopyFromJobList").data("kendoComboBox").value('');
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                }
            },
            error: function (request, status, error) {

            }
        });

        GetRegionalFieldsRegisterJobView(jobId);
    }
    function UpdateAccountCodeAmount()
    {
        var AccountCodeAmount = $("#AccountCodeAmount");
        var jobType = $('#JobType').data('kendoComboBox').value();
        if(jobType=="Salary" || jobType == '')
        {
            var total = Number($("#Amount").data("kendoNumericTextBox").value());
            AccountCodeAmount.val(total.toFixed(2));
        }
        else
        {
            var TotalHours = $("#TotalHours").data("FINSUITextInput").Value;
            var HourlyRate = $("#HourlyRate").data("kendoNumericTextBox").value();

            if (typeof TotalHours != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; (typeof HourlyRate != 'undefined')) {
                if ((TotalHours == '' || HourlyRate == '' || TotalHours == null || HourlyRate == null)) {
                    return;
                }
                total = Number(TotalHours) * Number(HourlyRate);
                AccountCodeAmount.val(total.toFixed(2));
            }
        }
    }
</script>

<script>
    function onRefreshAccountsPopup_PayrollAddJob(e) {
        e.sender.title('Account Code Allocation');
        e.sender.center();

        setFocusEventForKendoWindow('popupMultipleAccountCodeGrid_' + 'PayrollAddJob');
    }

    function onActivateAccountsPopup_PayrollAddJob() {
        if ($("#tbAccountCodeEdit_" + 'PayrollAddJob' + "acMultipleAccountCode").val() == '') {
            $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_" + 'PayrollAddJob' + "acMultipleAccountCode").removeAttr("disabled");
        }
    }

    function onCloseRefreshAccountCode_PayrollAddJob(e) {
        $("pupMultipleAccountCodeGrid_PayrollAddJob").html('');
        var stagingId = $("#AccountStagingId").val()
        var data = { stagingId: stagingId };

        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/GetAccountCode",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success == true) {
                    if (result.AccountCode) {
                        $.ajax({
                            cache: false,
                            url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/AcAccountTextBox",
                            data: { AccountCode: result.AccountCode, AccountType: 'Expenditure', EnableAccountMask: 'True', Key: 'PayrollAddJob' + 'acTextBox', AccountCodeWidthEm: "28", AllocationSequence: '0', AcAccountTextBoxOnChangeFunction: '' },
                            dataType: "html",
                            success: function (resp) {
                                $("#AccountCodeBox_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").html(resp);
                                if ('' !== '') {
                                    ;
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    }
                    //debugger;
                    $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").val(result.AccountCode);
                    if (result.AccountCode == "Multiple")
                        $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").select();
                }
            }
        });
    }
</script>

    <script>
        function btnOpenAccountCodeAssistant_PayrollAddJobacTextBox(e) {
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowAccountCodeAssistant_PayrollAddJobacTextBox")
                .SetIsModal(true)
                .SetTitle("Account Code Assistant")
                .SetonActivate(function () { AccountCodeLookUpActivated_PayrollAddJobacTextBox(); })
                .SetonDeactivate(function () { ReturnFromAccountCodeLookup_PayrollAddJobacTextBox(); });

            finsWindow.CreateWindow(false).SetHTMLContent('&lt;div id="divACL_PayrollAddJobacTextBox" &gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
            onAccountCodeLookupWindowOpen_PayrollAddJobacTextBox();
            finsWindow.OpenWindow();
            e.preventDefault();
        }

        $(function () {
            $("#btnOpenAccountCodeAssistant_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").click(btnOpenAccountCodeAssistant_PayrollAddJobacTextBox);
        });

        function onAccountCodeLookupWindowOpen_PayrollAddJobacTextBox(e) {
            var accountType = $("#hdnAccountTypeAcAccountTextBox_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").val();
            //If an account type is selected in account code assistant popup, use that account type.
            if (!$("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").val() &amp;&amp; $("#ACLAccountType_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox") &amp;&amp; $("#ACLAccountType_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox").Value) {
                accountType = $("#ACLAccountType_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox").Value;
            }
            var data = {
                AccountType: accountType,
                Key: "PayrollAddJobacTextBox",
                AccountCode: $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").val()
            };

            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                async: false,
                url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/AccountCodeLookup",
                data: data,
                success: function (result) {
                    $("#divACL_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").html(result);
                },
                error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                    console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
                }
            });
        }

        function AccountCodeLookUpActivated_PayrollAddJobacTextBox(e) {
            SelectedElementValues_PayrollAddJobacTextBox("tbAccountCodeEdit_" + 'PayrollAddJobacTextBox');
        }

        function ReturnFromAccountCodeLookup_PayrollAddJobacTextBox() {
            if (bOk) {
                bOk = false;
                var accountType
                var AccountId = $('#AccountId_PayrollAddJobacTextBox').data("kendoComboBox").value();

                if ($("#ACLAccountType_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").data("kendoComboBox") &amp;&amp; $("#ACLAccountType_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox").Value) {
                    accountType = $("#ACLAccountType_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox").Value;
                }
                else {
                    accountType = 'Expenditure';
                }
                $.ajax({
                    cache: false,
                    url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/AcAccountTextBox",
                    data: {
                        AccountCode: AccountId,
                        AccountType: accountType,
                        AccountCodeWidthEm: '28',
                        EnableAccountMask: 'True',
                        Key: 'PayrollAddJobacTextBox',
                        AcAccountTextBoxOnChangeFunction: '',
                        HtmlAttributeName: ''
                    },
                    dataType: "html",
                    success: function (resp) {
                        $("#AccountCodeBox_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").html(resp);
                        SetLabelDescriptionAccountCode('lblAccountDesc_PayrollAddJobacTextBox', AccountId);
                        if ('' !== '') {
                            ;
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        }
    </script>

<script>
    function AcMultipleAllocation_GetTotalAmount(unitsFN, unitPriceFN, amountFN, validate, precision) {
        var totalAmount = 0.0;

        if (amountFN != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; amountFN != '') {
            var amount = $("#" + amountFN).val();
            if (typeof amount != 'undefined') {
                if (validate &amp;&amp; (amount == '' || amount == '')) {
                    return null;
                }
                totalAmount = Number(amount);
            }
        }
        else {
            var orderQty = $("#" + unitsFN).val();
            var prUnitPrice = $("#" + unitPriceFN).val();
            if (typeof orderQty != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; (typeof prUnitPrice != 'undefined')) {
                if (validate &amp;&amp; (orderQty == '' || prUnitPrice == '' || orderQty == null || prUnitPrice == null)) {
                    return null;
                }
                totalAmount = Number(orderQty) * Number(prUnitPrice);
            }
        }

        return totalAmount.toFixed(precision);
    }

    function btnAccountcodeEditClick_PayrollAddJob(e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var key = 'PayrollAddJob';
        var dv = 'MultipleAccountCodeDataView1';
        var stgIdFN = 'AccountStagingId';
        var unitsFN = '';
        var unitPriceFN = '';
        var amountFN = 'AccountCodeAmount';
        var errFN = 'PayrollRegisterJobAdd_Error';
        var msg = 'Amount is required for Job Type Salary before account allocation\nHours/Days and Rate are required for Job Type Hourly/Daily before account allocation';
        var precision = 2;

        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", errFN);

        var accountCode = $('#tbAccountCodeEdit_' + key + 'acTextBox').val();
        var stagingId = $("#" + stgIdFN).val();
        var totalAmount = AcMultipleAllocation_GetTotalAmount(unitsFN, unitPriceFN, amountFN, true, precision);
        if (totalAmount == null || totalAmount == 'undefined') {
            ShowAjaxMessage(msg, "error", errFN);
            return;
        }

        var data = {
            accountCode: accountCode,
            stagingId: stagingId,
            Amount: totalAmount,
            dataview: dv,
            adjustAllocation: true,
                distributeStagingAmount: true,
            saveAllocationToUserSettings: true,
            acMultipleAccountCodeGrid: true,
            cycleId: '0'
        };
        var dataGrid = {
            DataView: 'MultipleAccountCodeDataView1',
            AccountStagingId: '0',
            Key: 'PayrollAddJob',
            AmountFieldName: 'AccountCodeAmount',
            TotalHoursFieldName: '',
            HourlyRateFieldName: '',
            AccountStagingIdFieldName: 'AccountStagingId',
            AccountType: 'Expenditure',
            IsViewOnly: 'False',
            CycleId: '0'
        };

        var height = ('False' === 'False' ? 500 : 420);
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/ProcessAccountCodeAllocation",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success == true) {
                    var modelKey = 'PayrollAddJob';
                    var accStagingId = (dataGrid.AccountStagingId == 0 ? (isNumber(result.StagingId) ? result.StagingId : 0) : dataGrid.AccountStagingId).toString();
                    dataGrid.AccountStagingId = accStagingId;
                    var w = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupMultipleAccountCodeGrid_" + modelKey)
                        .SetContent({
                            type: "POST",
                            url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/AcMultipleAccountCodeGrid",
                            data: dataGrid
                        })
                        .SetIsModal(true)
                        .SetWidth(960)
                        .SetHeight(height)
                        .IsRetainHeight(false)
                        .SetTitle("Account Code Allocation")
                        .SetonActivate(function () { eval("onActivateAccountsPopup_" + modelKey + "()"); })
                        .SetonClose(function (e) { if (w.GetDialogResult() != 'Cancel') eval("onCloseRefreshAccountCode_" + modelKey + "()"); });

                    $("#" + stgIdFN).val(result.StagingId);
                    $("#hdnAccountStagingIdEdit_" + key).val(result.StagingId);
                    $("#hdnAccountStagingId_MultipleAccountCodeGrid_" + key).val(result.StagingId);
                    $('#tbAccountCodeGrid_' + key).val('');
                    $("#tbAmountGrid_" + key).val('');

                    RemoveTabRestrictiononPopup();
                    setFocusEventForKendoWindow('popupMultipleAccountCodeGrid_' + key);
                    w.CreateWindow(true);
                    RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, key, key);
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", errFN);
                }
            }
        });
    }

    $(function () {
        $("#btnAccountcodeEdit_PayrollAddJob").click(btnAccountcodeEditClick_PayrollAddJob);
    });

    function showErrorMessageForAccountCodeEdit(message) {
        if ($("#" + 'PayrollRegisterJobAdd_Error') != null &amp;&amp; $("#" + 'PayrollRegisterJobAdd_Error') != '') {
            $("#" + 'PayrollRegisterJobAdd_Error').html(message);
            $("#" + 'PayrollRegisterJobAdd_Error').addClass("global_message error");
        }
        else {
            ShowAjaxMessage(message, "error");
        }
    }

<script>

    function GetRegionalFieldsRegisterJobView(jobSequence) {
        var employeeId = $("#SelectedEmployees").data("kendoComboBox").value();
        var jobId = jobSequence == null || jobSequence == '' || jobSequence==undefined? $("#JobName").data("kendoComboBox").value():jobSequence;
        var cycleId = $("#CycleId").val();
        var isSupp = $('#IsSupplemental').is(":checked");
        if (employeeId &lt; 0 || jobId &lt; 0) {
            $("#RegionalCustomFields").empty();
            $("#payrollJobAddCustomColumn").hide();
        }
        else
        {
            if ('10' &gt; 0) {
                var data = { employeeId: employeeId, jobSeq: jobId, cycleId: cycleId, isSupp: isSupp, pRRegId: '642' };
                $.ajax({
                    type: "POST",
                    async: false,
                    cache: false,
                    url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/GetCustomColumnsDetails",
                    data: data,
                    dataType: 'html',
                    success: function (result) {
                        if (result != null) {
                            $("#payrollJobAddCustomColumn").show();
                            $("#RegionalCustomFields").html(result);
                            var panelBar = $("#panelbarJobAdd").data("kendoPanelBar");

                            if ($("#panelbarJobAdd-2").css('display') === 'none') {
                                panelBar.expand($("#panelbarJobAdd-2")[0].parentElement);
                            }
                        }
                        else {
                            ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                        }
                    },
                    error: function (request, status, error) {

                    }
                });
            }
		}
		  var data = {
			  masterPositionId: jobId
        };
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/GetDataByPositionId',
            cache: false,
            data: data,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            success: function (result) {
                if(result.Success)
                    SetValues(true,result.dc);
            }
        });
    }
	function SetValues(masterPositionChanged, result, data, stepChange) {

		
		   $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox").SetValue(result.AccountCode);
		   $("#hdnAccountTypeAcAccountTextBox_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").val(result.StagingId);
			$("#AccountStagingId").val(result.StagingId);
			if (result.AccountCode != 'Multiple') {
				SetLabelDescriptionAccountCode('lblAccountDesc_PayrollAddJobacTextBox', result.AccountCode);
			}
			//JobType
			if (result.MasterPositionType != null &amp;&amp; result.MasterPositionType != '') {
				$("#JobType").data("FINSComboBox").SetValue(result.MasterPositionType);
				OnJobTypeChange();
			}				
			//Hourly Rate
			if (result.HourlyRate != null &amp;&amp; result.HourlyRate != '')
				$("#HourlyRate").data('FINSUINumberInput').SetValue(result.HourlyRate);
			//Hours PEr day
			if (result.HoursPerDay != null &amp;&amp; result.HoursPerDay != '')
				$("#TotalHours").data('FINSUITextInput').SetValue(result.HoursPerDay);			
		
			
			$("#Amount").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetValue(result.Salary);
			UpdateAccountCodeAmount();
					

	

	}

    function CancelRegisterJob() {
        var id = Number($("#AccountStagingId").val());

        if (id &gt; 0) {
            var data = {
                AccountStagingId: id
            };

            $.ajax({
                url: '/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/CancelJobRegister',
                cache: false,
                dataType: 'JSON',
                success: function (result) {
                }
            });
        }
        $("#popupWindowJobAdd").data("kendoWindow").close();
    }

    function EnableDisableControls() {
        if ($('#IsSupplemental').is(":checked") == false) {
            $('#NewSupplementalPay').data('kendoComboBox').enable(false);
            $('#JobType').data('kendoComboBox').enable(false);
            $('#TotalHours').disable();
            $('#HourlyRate').data("kendoNumericTextBox").enable(false);
            $('#Amount').data("kendoNumericTextBox").enable(false);
            $('#Comments').disable();
            var ddlCopyFromJobList = $("#CopyFromJobList").data("kendoComboBox");
            ddlCopyFromJobList.enable(false);

            $("label[for='NewSupplementalPay']").removeClass("RequiredLabel");
            $("label[for='JobType']").removeClass("RequiredLabel");
            $("label[for='TotalHours']").removeClass("RequiredLabel");
            $("label[for='HourlyRate']").removeClass("RequiredLabel");
            $("label[for='Amount']").removeClass("RequiredLabel");

            if($("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").data("kendoComboBox")!=='' &amp;&amp; $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").data("kendoComboBox") !== undefined)
            {
                $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").data("kendoComboBox").enable(false);
                $("#lblAccountCodeGridEdit_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").removeClass("RequiredLabel");
                $("#btnOpenAccountCodeAssistant_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").hide();
                $("#btnAccountcodeEdit_PayrollAddJob").hide();
            }
        }
        else {
            //enable all controls
            $('#NewSupplementalPay').data('kendoComboBox').enable(true);
            $('#JobType').data('kendoComboBox').enable(true);
            $('#TotalHours').enable();
            $('#HourlyRate').data("kendoNumericTextBox").enable(true);
            $('#Amount').data("kendoNumericTextBox").enable(true);
            $('#Comments').enable();

            $("label[for='NewSupplementalPay']").addClass("RequiredLabel");
            $("label[for='JobType']").addClass("RequiredLabel");
            $("label[for='TotalHours']").addClass("RequiredLabel");
            $("label[for='HourlyRate']").addClass("RequiredLabel");
            $("label[for='Amount']").addClass("RequiredLabel");
            var ddlCopyFromJobList = $("#CopyFromJobList").data("kendoComboBox");
            ddlCopyFromJobList.enable(true);
            if($("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").data("kendoComboBox") !=='' &amp;&amp; $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").data("kendoComboBox") !== undefined)
            {
                $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").data("kendoComboBox").enable(true);
                $("#lblAccountCodeGridEdit_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").addClass("RequiredLabel");
                $("#btnOpenAccountCodeAssistant_PayrollAddJobacTextBox").show();
                $("#btnAccountcodeEdit_PayrollAddJob").show();
            }
        }
    }

    $("#btnSave__PayrolRegisterJobEditDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        btnSave__PayrollRegisterJob(e);
    });

    $("#btnSaveAndAdd__PayrolRegisterJobEditDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PayrollRegisterJobAdd_Error");
        SaveRegisterJob(true, e);
    });

    $("#btnCancel__PayrolRegisterJobEditDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        CancelRegisterJob();
    });

    function SaveRegisterJob(addAnother, e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PayrollRegisterJobAdd_Error");
        var form = $("#FormPayrollRegisterJob");
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/SavePayrollJob",
            data: form.serialize(),
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {

                    if (addAnother) {
                        var grid = $("#PayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
                        if (!$("#divPayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("AptaDataView").OnlyOneItemSelected()) {
                            data = { id: "642~0" };
                        }
                        else {
                            data = { id: '642' + "~" + selectedRowIds.split('~')[1] };
                        }
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "PayrollRegisterJobAdd_Error");
                        destroyACMultipleAllocationWindows("PayrollAddJob");
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/Payroll/RegisterJob", data: data, type: "POST" });
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                    }
                    else {
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow").close();
                        var grid = $("#PayrollJobsAddendaDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        if (grid !== null &amp;&amp; grid !== undefined) {
                            grid.dataSource.read();
                        }
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                    }
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PayrollRegisterJobAdd_Error");
                }

            }
        });
    }

    function btnSave__PayrollRegisterJob(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PayrollRegisterJobAdd_Error");
        SaveRegisterJob(false, e);

    }
    function OnSupplmentalChange() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        var ddlSelectedEmployees = $("#SelectedEmployees").data("FINSComboBox");

        $("#SelectedEmployees").data("kendoComboBox").value('');
        ddlSelectedEmployees.DataParameters.CycleId = '5';
        ddlSelectedEmployees.DataParameters.IsSupplemental = $('#IsSupplemental').is(":checked");
        ddlSelectedEmployees.DataParameters.PayrollRegisterId = '642';
        ddlSelectedEmployees.ReloadData();

        var ddlJobName = $("#JobName").data("FINSComboBox");

        var employeeId = $("#SelectedEmployees").data("kendoComboBox").value() == "[All Employees]" ? -1 : $("#SelectedEmployees").data("kendoComboBox").value();

        $("#JobName").data("kendoComboBox").value('');

        ddlJobName.DataParameters.CycleId = '5';
        ddlJobName.DataParameters.IsSupplemental = $('#IsSupplemental').is(":checked");
        ddlJobName.DataParameters.EmployeeId = employeeId;
        ddlJobName.DataParameters.PayrollRegisterId = '642';
        ddlJobName.ReloadData();

        EnableDisableControls();
    }

    $('#IsSupplemental').on("click", OnSupplmentalChange);

    function HideShowJobTypePanels() {
        var jobType = $('#JobType').data('kendoComboBox').value();
        if (jobType == "Hourly") {
            if ($('#Amount').data("kendoNumericTextBox") !== null &amp;&amp; typeof $('#Amount').data("kendoNumericTextBox") !== "undefined")
                $('#Amount').data("kendoNumericTextBox").value("")

            $('#divPayrollHourly').show();
            $('#divPayrollSalary').hide();

        }
        else if (jobType == "Daily") {
            if ($('#Amount').data("kendoNumericTextBox") !== null &amp;&amp; typeof $('#Amount').data("kendoNumericTextBox") !== "undefined")
                $('#Amount').data("kendoNumericTextBox").value("")

            $('#divPayrollHourly').show();
            $('#divPayrollSalary').hide();
        }
        else {
            if ($('#TotalHours') !== null &amp;&amp; typeof $('#TotalHours') !== "undefined")
                $('#TotalHours').val("");

            if ($('#HourlyRate').data("kendoNumericTextBox") !== null &amp;&amp; typeof $('#HourlyRate').data("kendoNumericTextBox") !== "undefined")
                $('#HourlyRate').data("kendoNumericTextBox").value("");

            $('#divPayrollHourly').hide();
            $('#divPayrollSalary').show();
        }
    }

    function pageLoad() {
        EnableDisableControls();
        HideShowJobTypePanels();
        var jobTypeSelected = $('#JobType').data('kendoComboBox').value();
        if (jobTypeSelected != null || jobTypeSelected != '') {
            $('#divPayrollSalary').show();
            $('#divPayrollHourly').hide();
        }
        GetRegionalFieldsRegisterJobView();
        document.getElementById('AccountCode__RegisterJob').appendChild(document.getElementById('AccountCode__RegisterJobCotainer'));
    }

    $(document).ready(function () {

        pageLoad();

    });
</script>

    function FixIE10Content() {
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("top", parseFloat(50) + "px");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("bottom", parseFloat(65) + "px");
    }
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var popUp = $(".FINSWindowcontainer").closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow");
        if (popUp !== undefined) {
            var browser = get_browser();
            if (browser.name == 'MSIE' &amp;&amp; (browser.version == 10)) {
                FixIE10Content();
            }
            else {
                $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "relative");
            }
        }

    })
